grace period\\n310: \\tthresholds = thresholdsMet(thresholds, observations, false)\\n311: \\tdebugLogThresholdsWithObservation(\\\"thresholds - ignoring grace period\\\", thresholds, observations)\\n312: \\n313: \\t// determine the set of thresholds previously met that have not yet satisfied the associated min-reclaim\\n314: \\tif len(m.thresholdsMet) > 0 {\\n315: \\t\\tthresholdsNotYetResolved := thresholdsMet(m.thresholdsMet, observations, true)\\n316: \\t\\tthresholds = mergeThresholds(thresholds, thresholdsNotYetResolved)\\n317: \\t}\\n318: \\tdebugLogThresholdsWithObservation(\\\"thresholds - reclaim not satisfied\\\", thresholds, observations)\\n319: \\n320: \\t// track when a threshold was first observed\\n321: \\tnow := m.clock.Now()\\n322: \\tthresholdsFirstObservedAt := thresholdsFirstObservedAt(thresholds, m.thresholdsFirstObservedAt, now)\\n323: \\n324: \\t// the set of node conditions that are triggered by currently observed thresholds\\n325: \\tnodeConditions := nodeConditions(thresholds)\\n326: \\tif len(nodeConditions) > 0 {\\n327: \\t\\tklog.V(3).InfoS(\\\"Eviction manager: node conditions - observed\\\", \\\"nodeCondition\\\", nodeConditions)\\n328: \\t}\\n329: \\n330: \\t// track when a node condition was last observed\\n331: \\tnodeConditionsLastObservedAt := nodeConditionsLastObservedAt(nodeConditions, m.nodeConditionsLastObservedAt, now)\\n332: \\n333: \\t// node conditions report true if it has been observed within the transition period window\\n334: \\tnodeConditions = nodeConditionsObservedSince(nodeConditionsLastObservedAt, m.config.PressureTransitionPeriod, now)\\n335: \\tif len(nodeConditions) > 0 {\\n336: \\t\\tklog.V(3).InfoS(\\\"Eviction manager: node conditions - transition period not met\\\", \\\"nodeCondition\\\", nodeConditions)\\n337: \\t}\\n338: \\n339: \\t// determine the set of thresholds we need to drive eviction behavior (i.e. all grace periods are met)\\n340: \\tthresholds = thresholdsMetGracePeriod(thresholdsFirstObservedAt, now)\\n341: \\tdebugLogThresholdsWithObservation(\\\"thresholds - grace periods satisfied\\\", thresholds, observations)\\n342: \\n343: \\t// update internal state\\n344: \\tm.Lock()\\n345: \\tm.nodeConditions = nodeConditions\\n346: \\tm.thresholdsFirstObservedAt = thresholdsFirstObservedAt\\n347: \\tm.nodeConditionsLastObservedAt = nodeConditionsLastObservedAt\\n348: \\tm.thresholdsMet = thresholds\\n349: \\n350: \\t// determine the set of thresholds whose stats have been updated since the last sync\\n351: \\tthresholds = thresholdsUpdatedStats(thresholds, observations, m.lastObservations)\\n352: \\tdebugLogThresholdsWithObservation(\\\"thresholds - updated stats\\\", thresholds, observations)\\n353: \\n354: \\tm.lastObservations = observations\\n355: \\tm.Unlock()\\n356: \\n357: \\t// evict pods if there is a resource usage violation from local volume temporary storage\\n358: \\t// If eviction happens in localStorageEviction function, skip the rest of eviction action\\n359: \\tif m.localStorageCapacityIsolation {\\n360: \\t\\tif evictedPods := m.localStorageEviction(activePods, statsFunc); len(evictedPods) > 0 {\\n361: \\t\\t\\treturn evictedPods, nil\\n362: \\t\\t}\\n363: \\t}\\n364: \\n365: \\tif len(thresholds) == 0 {\\n366: \\t\\tklog.V(3).InfoS(\\\"Eviction manager: no resources are starved\\\")\\n367: \\t\\treturn nil, nil\\n368: \\t}\\n369: \\n370: \\t// rank the thresholds by eviction priority\\n371: \\tsort.Sort(byEvictionPriority(thresholds))\\n372: \\tthresholdToReclaim, resourceToReclaim, foundAny := getReclaimableThreshold(thresholds)\\n373: \\tif !foundAny {\\n374: \\t\\treturn nil, nil\\n375: \\t}\\n376: \\tklog.InfoS(\\\"Eviction manager: attempting to reclaim\\\", \\\"resourceName\\\", resourceToReclaim)\\n377: \\n378: \\t// record an event about the resources we are now attempting to reclaim via eviction\\n379: \\tm.recorder.Eventf(m.nodeRef, v1.EventTypeWarning, \\\"EvictionThresholdMet\\\", \\\"Attempting to reclaim %s\\\", resourceToReclaim)\\n380: \\n381: \\t// {\\n383: \\t\\tklog.InfoS(\\\"Eviction manager: able to reduce resource pressure without evicting pods.\\\", \\\"resourceName\\\", resourceToReclaim)\\n384: \\t\\treturn nil, nil\\n385: \\t}\\n386: \\n387: \\tklog.InfoS(\\\"Eviction manager: must evict pod(s) to reclaim\\\", \\\"resourceName\\\", resourceToReclaim)\\n388: \\n389: \\t// rank the pods for eviction\\n390: \\trank, ok := m.signalToRankFunc[thresholdToReclaim.Signal]\\n391: \\tif !ok {\\n392: \\t\\tklog.ErrorS(nil, \\\"Eviction manager: no ranking function for signal\\\", \\\"threshold\\\", thresholdToReclaim.Signal)\\n393: \\t\\treturn nil, nil\\n394: \\t}\\n395: \\n396: \\t// the only candidates viable for eviction are those pods that had anything running.\\n397: \\tif len(activePods) == 0 {\\n398: \\t\\tklog.ErrorS(nil, \\\"Eviction manager: eviction thresholds have been met, but no pods are active to evict\\\")\\n399: \\t\\treturn nil, nil\\n400: \\t}\\n401: \\n402: \\t// rank the running pods for eviction for the specified resource\\n403: \\trank(activePods, statsFunc)\\n404: \\n405: \\tklog.InfoS(\\\"Eviction manager: pods ranked for eviction\\\", \\\"pods\\\", klog.KObjSlice(activePods))\\n406: \\n407: \\t//record age of metrics for met thresholds that we are using for evictions.\\n408: \\tfor _, t := range thresholds {\\n409: \\t\\ttimeObserved := *pod.Spec.TerminationGracePeriodSeconds)\\n423: \\t\\t\\t}\\n424: \\t\\t}\\n425: \\n426: \\t\\tmessage, annotations := evictionMessage(resourceToReclaim, pod, statsFunc, thresholds, \t\t}\n303: \t}\n304: \n305: \t// make observations and get a function to derive pod usage stats relative to those observations.\n306: \tobservations, statsFunc := *managerImpl) waitForPodsCleanup(podCleanedUpFunc PodCleanedUpFunc, pods []*v1.Pod) {\n443: \ttimeout := m.clock.NewTimer(podCleanupTimeout)\n444: \tdefer timeout.Stop()\n445: \tticker := \t\t\t\t\treturn\n460: \t\t\t\t}\n461: \t\t\t}\n462: \t\t}\n463: \t}\n464: }\n465: \n466: // reclaimNodeLevelResources attempts to reclaim node level resources.  returns true if thresholds were satisfied and no pod eviction is required.\n467: func (m *managerImpl) reclaimNodeLevelResources(ctx context.Context, signalToReclaim evictionapi.Signal, resourceToReclaim v1.ResourceName) bool {\n468: \tnodeReclaimFuncs := m.signalToNodeReclaimFuncs[signalToReclaim]\n469: \tfor _, nodeReclaimFunc := range nodeReclaimFuncs {\n470: \t\t// attempt to reclaim the pressured resource.\n471: determine whether it exceeds the specified limit and needs\n500: // to be evicted. It also checks every container in the pod, if the container overlay usage exceeds the limit, the pod will be evicted too.\n501: func (m *managerImpl) localStorageEviction(pods []*v1.Pod, statsFunc statsFunc) []*v1.Pod {\n502: \tevicted := []*v1.Pod{}\n503: \tfor _, pod := range pods {\n504: \t\tpodStats, ok := statsFunc(pod)\n505: \t\tif !ok {\n506: \t\t\tcontinue\n507: \t\t}\n508: \n509: make(map[string]*resource.Quantity)\n529: \tfor _, volume := range podStats.VolumeStats {\n530: \t\tpodVolumeUsed[volume.Name] = resource.NewQuantity(int64(*volume.UsedBytes), resource.BinarySI)\n531: \t}\n532: \tfor i := range pod.Spec.Volumes {\n533: \t\tsource := &pod.Spec.Volumes[i].VolumeSource\n534: \t\tif source.EmptyDir != nil {\n535: \t\t\tsize := source.EmptyDir.SizeLimit\n536: \t\t\tused := podVolumeUsed[pod.Spec.Volumes[i].Name]\n537: \t\t\tif used != nil && size != nil && size.Sign() == 1 && used.Cmp(*size) > 0 {\n538: \t\t\t\t// the emptyDir usage exceeds the size limit, evict the pod\n539: \t\t\t\tif m.evictPod(pod, immediateEvictionGracePeriodSeconds, fmt.Sprintf(emptyDirMessageFmt, pod.Spec.Volumes[i].Name, size.String()), nil, nil) {\n540: \t\t\t\t\tmetrics.Evictions.WithLabelValues(signalEmptyDirFsLimit).Inc()\n541: \t\t\t\t\treturn true\n542: \t\t\t\t}\n543: \t\t\t\treturn false\n544: \t\t\t}\n545: \t\t}\n546: \t}\n547: \n548: \treturn false\n549: }\n550: \n551: func (m *managerImpl) podEphemeralStorageLimitEviction(podStats statsapi.PodStats, pod *v1.Pod) bool {\n552: \tpodLimits := resourcehelper.PodLimits(pod, ephemeral storage usage (container, emptyDir, host[etc-hosts, logs])\n559: \tpodEphemeralStorageTotalUsage := &resource.Quantity{}\n560: \tif podStats.EphemeralStorage != nil && podStats.EphemeralStorage.UsedBytes != nil {\n561: \t\tpodEphemeralStorageTotalUsage = resource.NewQuantity(int64(*podStats.EphemeralStorage.UsedBytes), resource.BinarySI)\n562: \t}\n563: size limit of containers, evict the pod\n566: \t\tmessage := fmt.Sprintf(podEphemeralStorageMessageFmt, podEphemeralStorageLimit.String())\n567: \t\tif m.evictPod(pod, immediateEvictionGracePeriodSeconds, message, nil, nil) {\n568: \t\t\tmetrics.Evictions.WithLabelValues(signalEphemeralPodFsLimit).Inc()\n569: \t\t\treturn true\n570: \t\t}\n571: \t\treturn false\n572: \t}\n573: \treturn false\n574: }\n575: \n576: func (m *managerImpl) containerEphemeralStorageLimitEviction(podStats statsapi.PodStats, pod *v1.Pod) bool {\n577: \tthresholdsMap := make(map[string]*resource.Quantity)\n578: \tfor _, container := range pod.Spec.Containers {\n579: \t\tephemeralLimit := container.Resources.Limits.StorageEphemeral()\n580: \t\tif ephemeralLimit != nil && ephemeralLimit.Value() != 0 {\n581: \t\t\tthresholdsMap[container.Name] = ephemeralLimit\n582: \t\t}\n583: \t}\n584: \n585: \tfor _, containerStat := range podStats.Containers {\n586: ephemeralStorageThreshold, ok := thresholdsMap[containerStat.Name]; ok {\n592: \t\t\tif ephemeralStorageThreshold.Cmp(*containerUsed) < 0 {\n593: \t\t\t\tif m.evictPod(pod, len(statements) == 0 {\n355: \t\treturn nil, nil\n356: \t}\n357: \tresults := []evictionapi.Threshold{}\n358: \tfor signal, val := range statements {\n359: \t\tresult, err := be ignored.\n372: func parseThresholdStatement(signal evictionapi.Signal, val string) (*evictionapi.Threshold, error) {\n373: \tif !validSignal(signal) {\n374: \t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(unsupportedEvictionSignal, signal)\n375: \t}\n376: \toperator := evictionapi.OpForSignal[signal]\n377: \tif strings.HasSuffix(val, \"%\") {\n378: \t\t// ignore 0% and 100%\n379: \t\tif val == \"0%\" || val == \"100%\" {\n380: \t\t\treturn nil, nil\n381: \t\t}\n382: \t\tpercentage, err := parsePercentage(val)\n383: \t\tif err != nil {\n384: \t\t\treturn nil, err\n385: \t\t}\n386: \t\tif percentage < 0 {\n387: \t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"eviction percentage threshold %v must be >= 0%%: %s\", signal, val)\n388: \t\t}\n389: \t\t// percentage is a float and should not be greater than 1 (100%)\n390: \t\tif percentage > 1 {\n391: \t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"eviction percentage threshold %v must be <= 100%%: %s\", signal, val)\n392: \t\t}\n393: \t\treturn &evictionapi.Threshold{\n394: \t\t\tSignal:   signal,\n395: \t\t\tOperator: operator,\n396: \t\t\tValue: evictionapi.ThresholdValue{\n397: \t\t\t\tPercentage: percentage,\n398: \t\t\t},\n399: \t\t}, nil, fmt.Errorf(\"eviction threshold %v must be positive: %s\", signal, &quantity)\n407: \t}\n408: \treturn &evictionapi.Threshold{\n409: \t\tSignal:   signal,\n410: \t\tOperator: operator,\n411: \t\tValue: evictionapi.ThresholdValue{\n412: \t\t\tQuantity: &quantity,\n413: \t\t},\n414: \t}, nil\n415: }\n416: \n417: // parsePercentage parses a string representing a percentage value\n418: func parsePercentage(input string) (float32, error) {\n419: \tvalue, err := strconv.ParseFloat(strings.TrimRight(input, \"%\"), 32)\n420: \tif err != nil {\n421: \t\treturn 0, err\n422: \t}\n423: \treturn float32(value) / 100, nil\n424: }\n425: \n426: // parseGracePeriods parses the grace period statements\n427: func parseGracePeriods(statements map[string]string) (map[evictionapi.Signal]time.Duration, \t}\n454: \tresults := map[evictionapi.Signal]evictionapi.ThresholdValue{}\n455: \tfor signal, val := range statements {\n456: \t\tsignal := evictionapi.Signal(signal)\n457: \t\tif \t}\n484: \treturn results, nil\n485: }\n486: \n487: // diskUsage converts used bytes into a resource quantity.\n488: func diskUsage(fsStats *statsapi.FsStats) *resource.Quantity {\n489: \tif fsStats and returns:\n614: //\n615: //\t-1 if p1 <  p2\n616: //\t 0 if p1 == p2\n617: //\t+1 if p1 >  p2\n618: type cmpFunc func(p1, p2 *v1.Pod) int\n619: \n620: // multiSorter implements the Sort interface, sorting changes within.\n621: type multiSorter struct {\n622: \tpods []*v1.Pod\n623: \tcmp  []cmpFunc\n624: }\n625: \n626: // Sort sorts the argument slice according to the less functions passed to OrderedBy.\n627: func (ms *multiSorter) Sort(pods []*v1.Pod) {\n628: \tms.pods = pods\n629: \tsort.Sort(ms)\n630: }\n631: \n632: // OrderedBy returns a Sorter that sorts using the cmp functions, in order.\n633: // Call its Sort method to sort the data.\n634: func orderedBy(cmp ...cmpFunc) *multiSorter {\n635: \treturn &multiSorter{\n636: \t\tcmp: cmp,\n637: \t}\n638: }\n639: \n640: // Len is part of sort.Interface.\n641: func (ms *multiSorter) Len() int {\n642: \treturn len(ms.pods)\n643: }\n644: \n645: // Swap is part of sort.Interface.\n646: func (ms *multiSorter) Swap(i, j int) {\n647: \tms.pods[i], ms.pods[j] = ms.pods[j], ms.pods[i]\n648: }\n649: \n650: // Less is part of sort.Interface.\n651: func (ms *multiSorter) Less(i, j int) bool {\n652: \tp1, p2 := ms.pods[i], ms.pods[j]\n653: \tvar k int\n654: \tfor k = 0; k < len(ms.cmp)-1; k++ {\n655: \t\tcmpResult := ms.cmp[k](p1, p2)\n656: \t\t// p1 is less than p2\n657: \t\tif cmpResult < 0 {\n658: \t\t\treturn true\n659: \t\t}\n660: \t\t// p1 is greater than p2\n661: \t\tif cmpResult > 0 {\n662: \t\t\treturn false\n663: \t\t}\n664: \t\t// we don't know yet\n665: \t}\n666: \t// the last cmp func is the final decider\n667: \treturn ms.cmp[k](p1, p2) < 0\n668: }\n669: \n670: // priority compares pods by Priority, if priority is enabled.\n671: func priority(p1, p2 *v1.Pod) int {\n672: \tpriority1 := corev1helpers.PodPriority(p1)\n673: \tpriority2 := corev1helpers.PodPriority(p2)\n674: \tif priority1 == priority2 {\n675: \t\treturn 0\n676: \t}\n677: \tif priority1 > priority2 {\n678: \t\treturn 1\n679: \t}\n680: \treturn -1\n681: }\n682: \n683: // exceedMemoryRequests compares whether or not pods' memory usage exceeds their requests\n684: func exceedMemoryRequests(stats statsFunc) cmpFunc {\n685: \treturn func(p1, p2 *v1.Pod) int {\n686: \t\tp1Stats, p1Found := stats(p1)\n687: \t\tp2Stats, p2Found := stats(p2)\n688: \t\tif !p1Found || !p2Found {\n689: \t\t\t// prioritize evicting the pod for which no stats were found\n690: \t\t\treturn cmpBool(!p1Found, !p2Found)\n691: \t\t}\n692: \n693: \t\tp1Memory := memoryUsage(p1Stats.Memory)\n694: \t\tp2Memory := memoryUsage(p2Stats.Memory)\n695: \t\tp1ExceedsRequests := p1Memory.Cmp(v1resource.GetResourceRequestQuantity(p1, v1.ResourceMemory)) == 1\n696: \t\tp2ExceedsRequests := p2Memory.Cmp(v1resource.GetResourceRequestQuantity(p2, v1.ResourceMemory)) == 1\n697: \t\t// prioritize evicting the pod which exceeds its requests\n698: \t\treturn cmpBool(p1ExceedsRequests, p2ExceedsRequests)\n699: \t}\n700: }\n701: \n702: // memory compares pods by largest consumer of memory relative to request.\n703: func memory(stats statsFunc) cmpFunc {\n704: \treturn func(p1, p2 *v1.Pod) int {\n705: \t\tp1Stats, p1Found := stats(p1)\n706: \t\tp2Stats, p2Found := stats(p2)\n707: \t\tif !p1Found || !p2Found {\n708: \t\t\t// prioritize evicting the pod for which no stats were found\n709: \t\t\treturn cmpBool(!p1Found, !p2Found)\n710: \t\t}\n711: \n712: \t\t// adjust p1, p2 usage relative to the request (if any)\n713: \t\tp1Memory := memoryUsage(p1Stats.Memory)\n714: \t\tp1Request := v1resource.GetResourceRequestQuantity(p1, v1.ResourceMemory)\n715: \t\tp1Memory.Sub(p1Request)\n716: \n717: \t\tp2Memory := memoryUsage(p2Stats.Memory)\n718: \t\tp2Request := v1resource.GetResourceRequestQuantity(p2, v1.ResourceMemory)\n719: \t\tp2Memory.Sub(p2Request)\n720: \n721: \t\t// prioritize evicting the pod which has the larger consumption of memory\n722: \t\treturn p2Memory.Cmp(*p1Memory)\n723: \t}\n724: }\n725: \n726: // process compares pods by largest consumer of process number relative to request.\n727: func process(stats statsFunc) cmpFunc {\n728: \treturn func(p1, p2 *v1.Pod) int {\n729: \t\tp1Stats, p1Found := stats(p1)\n730: \t\tp2Stats, p2Found := stats(p2)\n731: \t\tif !p1Found || !p2Found {\n732: \t\t\t// prioritize evicting the pod for which no stats were found\n733: \t\t\treturn cmpBool(!p1Found, !p2Found)\n734: \t\t}\n735: \n736: \t\tp1Process := processUsage(p1Stats.ProcessStats)\n737: \t\tp2Process := processUsage(p2Stats.ProcessStats)\n738: \t\treturn int(p2Process - p1Process)\n739: \t}\n740: }\n741: \n742: // exceedDiskRequests compares whether or not pods' disk usage exceeds their requests\n743: func exceedDiskRequests(stats statsFunc, fsStatsToMeasure []fsStatsType, diskResource v1.ResourceName) cmpFunc {\n744: \treturn func(p1, p2 *v1.Pod) int {\n745: \t\tp1Stats, p1Found := !p2Found)\n750: \t\t}\n751: \n752: \t\tp1Usage, p1Err := podDiskUsage(p1Stats, p1, fsStatsToMeasure)\n753: \t\tp2Usage, p2Err := podDiskUsage(p2Stats, p2, fsStatsToMeasure)\n754: \t\tif p1Err != nil || p2Err != nil {\n755: \t\t\t// prioritize evicting the pod which had an error getting stats\n756: \t\t\treturn cmpBool(p1Err != nil, p2Err != nil)\n757: \t\t}\n758: \n759: \t\tp1Disk := p2Disk.Cmp(v1resource.GetResourceRequestQuantity(p2, diskResource)) == 1\n763: \t\t// prioritize evicting the pod which exceeds its requests\n764: \t\treturn cmpBool(p1ExceedsRequests, p2ExceedsRequests)\n765: \t}\n766: }\n767: \n768: // disk compares pods by largest consumer of disk relative to request for the specified disk resource.\n769: func disk(stats statsFunc, 0\n800: \t}\n801: \tif !b {\n802: \t\treturn -1\n803: \t}\n804: \treturn 1\n805: }\n806: \n807: // rankMemoryPressure orders the input pods for eviction in response to memory pressure.\n808: // It ranks by whether or not the pod's usage exceeds its requests, then by priority, and\n809: // finally by memory usage above requests.\n810: func rankMemoryPressure(pods []*v1.Pod, stats statsFunc) {\n811: \torderedBy(exceedMemoryRequests(stats), priority, memory(stats)).Sort(pods)\n812: }\n813: \n814: // rankPIDPressure orders the input pods by priority in response to PID pressure.\n815: func rankPIDPressure(pods []*v1.Pod, stats statsFunc) {\n816: \torderedBy(priority, process(stats)).Sort(pods)\n817: }\n818: \n819: // rankDiskPressureFunc returns a rankFunc that measures the specified fs \t\torderedBy(exceedDiskRequests(stats, fsStatsToMeasure, diskResource), priority, disk(stats, fsStatsToMeasure, diskResource)).Sort(pods)\n823: \t}\n824: }\n825: \n826: // byEvictionPriority byEvictionPriority) Swap(i, j int) { a[i], a[j] = a[j], a[i] }\n831: \n832: // Less ranks memory before all other resources, and ranks thresholds with no resource to reclaim last\n833: func (a {\n935: \tresults := []evictionapi.Threshold{}\n936: \tfor i := range thresholds {\n937: \t\tthreshold := thresholds[i]\n938: \t\tobserved, found := observations[threshold.Signal]\n939: \t\tif !found Thresholds\\n\\nThe memory pressure eviction thresholds are defined in the `pkg/kubelet/eviction/` package in kubernetes/kubernetes:\\n\\n### Threshold Signals (pkg/kubelet/eviction/api/types.go)\\nTwo primary signals trigger memory-based evictions:\\n- `SignalMemoryAvailable` (constant: \\\"memory.available\\\") - Triggers eviction when available memory drops below threshold\\n- `SignalAllocatableMemoryAvailable` (constant: \\\"allocatableMemory.available\\\") - Triggers eviction based on allocatable memory available to pods\\n\\n### Default Thresholds\\nThe default memory pressure eviction thresholds vary by platform:\\n- **Linux** (pkg/kubelet/eviction/defaults_linux.go): `memory.available: 100Mi` - Kubelet will evict pods when less than 100MB of memory is available\\n- **Windows** (pkg/kubelet/eviction/defaults_windows.go): `memory.available: 500Mi` - Kubelet will evict pods when less than 500MB of memory is available\\n\\nThese defaults are stored in the `DefaultEvictionHard` map variable, which is used by the kubelet if no explicit eviction thresholds are configured.\\n\\n## Eviction Manager Decision Logic\\n\\n### Core Configuration (pkg/kubelet/eviction/types.go)\\nThe `Config` struct defines eviction parameters:\\n- `Thresholds []evictionapi.Threshold` - The set of conditions monitored to trigger eviction\\n- `PressureTransitionPeriod` - Duration to wait before transitioning out of a pressure condition\\n- `MaxPodGracePeriodSeconds` - Maximum allowed grace period when terminating pods\\n\\n### Main Control Loop (pkg/kubelet/eviction/eviction_manager.go)\\nThe `managerImpl` type implements the `Manager` interface with the critical `synchronize()` method that:\\n1. Gets current resource usage observations from the node\\n2. Compares observations against configured thresholds\\n3. Determines which thresholds are met using `thresholdsMet()` helper\\n4. Applies grace periods and tracks node conditions\\n5. Ranks pods for eviction using signal-specific ranking functions\\n6. Evicts the highest-priority pod by calling `evictPod()`\\n\\n### Threshold Evaluation (pkg/kubelet/eviction/helpers.go)\\nThe `thresholdsMet()` function evaluates each threshold:\\n- Retrieves observed available resource for the signal\\n- Compares against the threshold value: if `available < threshold`, threshold is met\\n- Returns list of met thresholds for the eviction manager to process\\n\\n### Pod Ranking for Memory Pressure (pkg/kubelet/eviction/helpers.go)\\nWhen memory pressure is detected, the `rankMemoryPressure()` function ranks pods for eviction by:\\n1. **Usage vs. Requests**: Pods exceeding memory requests come first\\n2. **Priority**: Higher priority pods are ranked lower (evicted last)\\n3. **Memory Usage Above Requests**: Pods with higher memory consumption above requests are evicted first\\n\\n### Eviction Signal Mapping (pkg/kubelet/eviction/helpers.go)\\nThe `buildSignalToRankFunc()` function maps memory signals to their ranking function:\\n- Both `SignalMemoryAvailable` and `SignalAllocatableMemoryAvailable` use `rankMemoryPressure()`\\n- This ensures consistent pod ranking behavior for both memory-based eviction signals\\n\\n## Complete Eviction Flow\\n\\nWhen a node experiences memory pressure:\\n1. The kubelet's eviction manager's `synchronize()` loop (running every ~10 seconds) collects memory statistics\\n2. Compares available memory against thresholds from config (default: 100Mi on Linux)\\n3. If memory.available < threshold, the `thresholdsMet()` function identifies this threshold as met\\n4. The `rankMemoryPressure()` function ranks active pods for eviction\\n5. The pod with highest eviction priority is selected and terminated via `evictPod()`\\n6. The pod's status is set to `PodFailed` with reason `\\\"Evicted\\\"` and a message indicating memory pressure\\n7. This process repeats until memory available rises above the threshold\\n\\n## Related Configuration\\n\\nThese mechanisms can be configured via kubelet flags:\\n- `--eviction-hard`: Hard eviction thresholds (e.g., `memory.available=100Mi`)\\n- `--eviction-soft`: Soft eviction thresholds with grace periods\\n- `--eviction-pressure-transition-period`: Duration before transitioning out of pressure condition\\n- `--eviction-max-pod-grace-period`: Maximum grace period for soft evictions\\n\\nThe eviction system works in conjunction with QoS class (Guaranteed, Burstable, BestEffort) to prioritize which pods get evicted under memory pressure.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":8,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1338,"cache_read_input_tokens":73805,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1338},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"e01d4f4a-8c60-402c-9424-bc02b984724f","uuid":"ff767706-c602-4275-89d5-06513182e9a0"}
